## Language references

## References for contextual rules
#
# RFC 5891: "Internationalized Domain Names in Applications (IDNA): Protocol" 
# (proposed standard), http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc5891
#
# RFC 5892: "The Unicode Code Points and Internationalized Domain Names for Applications 
# (IDNA)"  (proposed standard), http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc5892
#
# UAX#24 (Unicode Standard Annex #24), "Unicode Script Property", 
# http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr24
#
# Unicode Character Database "ScriptExtensions.txt", 
# http://www.unicode.org/Public/7.0.0/ucd/ScriptExtensions.txt  


## Code points requiring contextual rules
#
# Code point                        Description of rule/Reference
#
# U+002D                            Label must neither start nor end with U+002D. Label 
#   HYPHEN-MINUS                    must not have U+002D in both third and fourth
#                                   position. RFC 5891 (sec 4.2.3.1)
#
# U+3006                            Label must also have some Han, Hiragana or Katakana
#   IDEOGRAPHIC CLOSING MARK        code point. UAX #24 (sec 1.3) + Unicode Character
#                                   Database (ScriptExtensions.txt)
#
# U+30FB                            Label must also have some Han, Hiragana or Katakana
#   KATAKANA MIDDLE DOT             code point. RFC 5892 (Appendix A. 7.)
#
# U+30FC                            Label must also have some Hiragana or Katakana
#   KATAKANA-HIRAGANA PROLONGED     code point. UAX #24 (sec 1.3) + Unicode Character
#   SOUND MARK                      Database (ScriptExtensions.txt)
